- [🧠🌐 STANDING DIRECTIVE 2026-05-15 — *"i thought we had built autopilot as a metaconsumer of sorts / like as an interface to us and our trusted agent partner / kind of sitting between all of us / like a nervous system we have been building out facilitating continual learning"*. **Cathedral Autopilot is THE canonical nervous system / meta-consumer / human↔agent interface / continual-learning facilitator** — sits between (operator + Claude + codex partners) AND (substrate/dispatch infrastructure).
